;(() => {
  const initAdPosition = (adPositionsRef) => {
    if (window.cdaaas.helpers && window.cdaaas.helpers.adsSmartContainerSetup) {
      window.cdaaas.helpers.adsSmartContainerSetup(adPositionsRef)
    }

    if (window.libPubReady) {
      window.bannerLazyLoading('banner_sticky')
    } else {
      document.addEventListener('libPubReady', () => {
        window.bannerLazyLoading('banner_sticky')
      })
    }
  }

  const elementBanner = document.querySelector('banner_sticky')

  const adPositionsRef = [
    {
      name: 'banner_sticky',
      initialHeight: 50,
      forgotRuleEnabled: false,
      hasMultipleSize: true,
      querySelector: () => elementBanner
    }
  ]

  const contentType = window.utag_data.content_type
  const isSchedule = window.location.href.indexOf('agenda') > -1

  if (contentType === 'Tabela') {
    initAdPosition(adPositionsRef)
  } else if (contentType === 'Página' && isSchedule) {
    new CustomEvent('showBannerBanderole')
    document.addEventListener('showBannerBanderole', () => {
      const elBannerBanderoleWrapper = document.getElementById(
        'bannder_banderole_wrapper'
      )
      const bannerBettingBanderole =
        '<div class="banner_betting_banderole" id="banner_sticky"><div class="glb-skeleton-box--empty skeleton-betting"style="--skeleton-width: 100%; --skeleton-height: 50px; margin: 0 auto;"></div></div>'
      elBannerBanderoleWrapper.innerHTML = bannerBettingBanderole

      initAdPosition(adPositionsRef)
    })
